                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                    _DISPLAY
                LOOP
                DO
                    exitloop = 0
                    jukebox = _SNDOPEN(location$, "VOL, SYNC, LEN, PAUSE")
                    _SNDPLAY jukebox
                    DO
                        _LIMIT 64
                        CLS
                        PRINT " You are are currently listening to "; song$; "!"
                        length = _SNDLEN(jukebox)
                        minutes = INT((length / 60))
                        minutes$ = STR$(minutes)
                        minutes$ = LTRIM$(minutes$)
                        seconds = INT((length - (minutes * 60)))
                        seconds$ = STR$(seconds)
                        seconds$ = LTRIM$(seconds$)
                        digitseconds = LEN(seconds$)
                        IF digitseconds = 1 THEN
                            seconds$ = "0" + seconds$
                        END IF
                        position = _SNDGETPOS(jukebox)
                        playingminutes = INT((position / 60))
                        playingminutes$ = STR$(playingminutes)
                        playingminutes$ = LTRIM$(playingminutes$)
                        playingseconds = INT((position - (playingminutes * 60)))
                        playingseconds$ = STR$(playingseconds)
                        playingseconds$ = LTRIM$(playingseconds$)
                        playingdigitseconds = LEN(playingseconds$)
                        IF playingdigitseconds = 1 THEN
                            playingseconds$ = "0" + playingseconds$
                        END IF
                        timedisplay$ = " " + playingminutes$ + ":" + playingseconds$
                        totaltime$ = minutes$ + ":" + seconds$
                        PSET (10, 25)
                        DRAW "D14 R200 U14 L200"
                        barloc = _ROUND(((position / length) * 197))
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 33)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 33)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 33)
                        LOCATE 4, 2
                        PRINT timedisplay$
                        LOCATE 4, 23
                        PRINT totaltime$
                        PRINT
                        PRINT "What would you like to do?"
                        PRINT "     1-Pause song"
                        PRINT "     2-Play song"
                        PRINT "     3-Change Volume"
                        PRINT "     4-Restart song"
                        PRINT "     5-Replay this song"
                        PRINT "     6-Listen to another song"
                        PRINT "     7-Listen to this song and do other stuff"
                        PRINT "     8-Make this song your theme"
                        PRINT "     9-Exit"
                        pre = 1
                        GOSUB controls
                        IF k$ = CHR$(49) THEN
                            _SNDPAUSE jukebox
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
                            playing = _SNDPLAYING(jukebox)
                            IF playing = 0 THEN
                                _SNDPLAY jukebox
                            END IF
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(51) THEN
                            volume$ = ""
                            exitloop = 0
                            DO
                                decimal = 0
                                DO
                                    DO
                                        _LIMIT 64
                                        CLS
                                        PRINT "Enter a value between 0 and 1, with 1 being full volume"
                                        PRINT ": "; volume$
                                        pre = 1
                                        GOSUB controls
                                        IF k$ = CHR$(46) AND decimal = 0 THEN
                                            decimal = 1
                                            volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                            inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                            decimalloc = LEN(volume$)
                                        END IF
                                        IF k$ >= CHR$(48) AND k$ <= CHR$(58) THEN
                                            volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                            inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                        END IF
                                        IF k$ = CHR$(8) AND inputlength > 0 THEN
                                            volume$ = MID$(volume$, 1, (inputlength - 1))
                                            inputlength = (inputlength - 1)
                                            IF inputlength < decimalloc THEN
                                                decimal = 0
                                            END IF
                                        END IF
                                        _DISPLAY
                                    LOOP UNTIL k$ = CHR$(13)
                                    volume = VAL(volume$)
                                    IF volume < 0 OR volume > 1 THEN
                                        volume$ = ""
                                        inputlength = 0
                                        EXIT DO
                                    END IF
                                    _SNDVOL jukebox, volume
                                    exitloop = 1
                                    EXIT DO
                                LOOP
                                IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                            LOOP
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(52) THEN
                            _SNDSTOP jukebox
                            exitloop = 0
                            EXIT DO
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(53) THEN
                            playing = _SNDPLAYING(jukebox)
                            IF playing = 0 THEN
                                _SNDSTOP jukebox
                                exitloop = 0
                                EXIT DO
                            END IF
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(54) THEN
                            _SNDSTOP jukebox
                            exitloop = 1
                            EXIT DO
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(55) THEN
                            _SNDPAUSE jukebox
                            _SNDLOOP jukebox
                            GOTO BEGIN
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(56) AND nottheme = 0 THEN
                            theme$ = location$
                            filename$ = "user\pref\theme.txt"
                            userdata$ = location$
                            GOSUB encrypter
                            duotheme = 0
                            filename$ = "user\pref\duotheme.txt"
                            userdata$ = STR$(duotheme)
                            GOSUB encrypter
                            _SNDPAUSE jukebox
                            GOTO PREBEGIN
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(57) THEN
                            GOTO PREBEGIN
                        END IF
                        _DISPLAY
                    LOOP
                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                LOOP
            LOOP
        END IF
        IF k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
            DO
                _SNDCLOSE randomjukebox

                END SELECT
                DO
                    exitloop = 0
                    randomjukebox = _SNDOPEN(location$, "VOL, SYNC, LEN, PAUSE")
                    _SNDPLAY randomjukebox
                    DO
                        _LIMIT 64
                        CLS
                        PRINT " You are are currently listening to "; song$; "!"
                        length = _SNDLEN(randomjukebox)
                        minutes = INT((length / 60))
                        minutes$ = STR$(minutes)
                        minutes$ = LTRIM$(minutes$)
                        seconds = INT((length - (minutes * 60)))
                        seconds$ = STR$(seconds)
                        seconds$ = LTRIM$(seconds$)
                        digitseconds = LEN(seconds$)
                        IF digitseconds = 1 THEN
                            seconds$ = "0" + seconds$
                        END IF
                        position = _SNDGETPOS(randomjukebox)
                        playingminutes = INT((position / 60))
                        playingminutes$ = STR$(playingminutes)
                        playingminutes$ = LTRIM$(playingminutes$)
                        playingseconds = INT((position - (playingminutes * 60)))
                        playingseconds$ = STR$(playingseconds)
                        playingseconds$ = LTRIM$(playingseconds$)
                        playingdigitseconds = LEN(playingseconds$)
                        IF playingdigitseconds = 1 THEN
                            playingseconds$ = "0" + playingseconds$
                        END IF
                        timedisplay$ = " " + playingminutes$ + ":" + playingseconds$
                        totaltime$ = minutes$ + ":" + seconds$
                        PSET (10, 25)
                        DRAW "D14 R200 U14 L200"
                        barloc = _ROUND(((position / length) * 197))
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 33)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 33)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 33)
                        LOCATE 4, 2
                        PRINT timedisplay$
                        LOCATE 4, 23
                        PRINT totaltime$
                        PRINT
                        PRINT "What would you like to do?"
                        PRINT "     1-Pause song"
                        PRINT "     2-Play song"
                        PRINT "     3-Change Volume"
                        PRINT "     4-Restart song"
                        PRINT "     5-Replay this song"
                        PRINT "     6-Listen to another song"
                        PRINT "     7-Listen to this song and do other stuff"
                        PRINT "     8-Make this song your theme"
                        PRINT "     9-Exit"
                        pre = 1
                        GOSUB controls
                        IF k$ = CHR$(49) THEN
                            _SNDPAUSE randomjukebox
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
                            playing = _SNDPLAYING(randomjukebox)
                            IF playing = 0 THEN
                                _SNDPLAY randomjukebox
                            END IF
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(51) THEN
                            volume$ = ""
                            exitloop = 0
                            DO
                                decimal = 0
                                DO
                                    DO
                                        _LIMIT 64
                                        CLS
                                        PRINT "Enter a value between 0 and 1, with 1 being full volume"
                                        PRINT ": "; volume$
                                        pre = 1
                                        GOSUB controls
                                        IF k$ = CHR$(46) AND decimal = 0 THEN
                                            decimal = 1
                                            volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                            inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                            decimalloc = LEN(volume$)
                                        END IF
                                        IF k$ >= CHR$(48) AND k$ <= CHR$(58) THEN
                                            volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                            inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                        END IF
                                        IF k$ = CHR$(8) AND inputlength > 0 THEN
                                            volume$ = MID$(volume$, 1, (inputlength - 1))
                                            inputlength = (inputlength - 1)
                                            IF inputlength < decimalloc THEN
                                                decimal = 0
                                            END IF
                                        END IF
                                        _DISPLAY
                                    LOOP UNTIL k$ = CHR$(13)
                                    volume = VAL(volume$)
                                    IF volume < 0 OR volume > 1 THEN
                                        volume$ = ""
                                        inputlength = 0
                                        EXIT DO
                                    END IF
                                    _SNDVOL randomjukebox, volume
                                    exitloop = 1
                                    EXIT DO
                                LOOP
                                IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                            LOOP
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(52) THEN
                            _SNDSTOP randomjukebox
                            exitloop = 0
                            EXIT DO
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(53) THEN
                            playing = _SNDPLAYING(randomjukebox)
                            IF playing = 0 THEN
                                _SNDSTOP randomjukebox
                                exitloop = 0
                                EXIT DO
                            END IF
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(54) THEN
                            _SNDSTOP jukebox
                            exitloop = 1
                            EXIT DO
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(55) THEN
                            _SNDPAUSE randomjukebox
                            _SNDLOOP randomjukebox
                            GOTO BEGIN
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(56) AND nottheme = 0 THEN
                            theme$ = location$
                            filename$ = "user\pref\theme.txt"
                            userdata$ = location$
                            GOSUB encrypter
                            duotheme = 0
                            filename$ = "user\pref\duotheme.txt"
                            userdata$ = STR$(duotheme)
                            GOSUB encrypter
                            _SNDPAUSE randomjukebox
                            GOTO PREBEGIN
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(57) THEN
                            GOTO PREBEGIN
                        END IF
                        _DISPLAY
                    LOOP
                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                LOOP
            LOOP
        END IF
        IF k$ = CHR$(51) THEN
            DO
                _SNDCLOSE shufflejukebox

                DO
                    pause = 0
                    exitloop = 0
                    shufflejukebox = _SNDOPEN(location$, "VOL, SYNC, LEN, PAUSE")
                    _SNDPLAY shufflejukebox
                    DO
                        _LIMIT 64
                        CLS
                        PRINT " You are are currently listening to "; song$; "!"
                        PRINT " A new song will play automatically once the current song is finished"
                        length = _SNDLEN(shufflejukebox)
                        minutes = INT((length / 60))
                        minutes$ = STR$(minutes)
                        minutes$ = LTRIM$(minutes$)
                        seconds = INT((length - (minutes * 60)))
                        seconds$ = STR$(seconds)
                        seconds$ = LTRIM$(seconds$)
                        digitseconds = LEN(seconds$)
                        IF digitseconds = 1 THEN
                            seconds$ = "0" + seconds$
                        END IF
                        position = _SNDGETPOS(shufflejukebox)
                        playingminutes = INT((position / 60))
                        playingminutes$ = STR$(playingminutes)
                        playingminutes$ = LTRIM$(playingminutes$)
                        playingseconds = INT((position - (playingminutes * 60)))
                        playingseconds$ = STR$(playingseconds)
                        playingseconds$ = LTRIM$(playingseconds$)
                        playingdigitseconds = LEN(playingseconds$)
                        IF playingdigitseconds = 1 THEN
                            playingseconds$ = "0" + playingseconds$
                        END IF
                        timedisplay$ = " " + playingminutes$ + ":" + playingseconds$
                        totaltime$ = minutes$ + ":" + seconds$
                        PSET (10, 25)
                        DRAW "D14 R200 U14 L200"
                        barloc = _ROUND(((position / length) * 197))
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 10), 33)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 11), 33)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 31)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 32)
                        PSET ((barloc + 12), 33)
                        LOCATE 4, 2
                        PRINT timedisplay$
                        LOCATE 4, 23
                        PRINT totaltime$
                        PRINT
                        PRINT "What would you like to do?"
                        PRINT "     1-Pause song"
                        PRINT "     2-Play song"
                        PRINT "     3-Change Volume"
                        PRINT "     4-Skip this song"
                        PRINT "     5-Make this song your theme"
                        PRINT "     6-Exit"
                        pre = 1
                        GOSUB controls
                        IF k$ = CHR$(49) THEN
                            _SNDPAUSE shufflejukebox
                            pause = 1
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
                            playing = _SNDPLAYING(shufflejukebox)
                            IF playing = 0 THEN
                                _SNDPLAY shufflejukebox
                                pause = 0
                            END IF
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(51) THEN
                            volume$ = ""
                            exitloop = 0
                            DO
                                decimal = 0
                                DO
                                    DO
                                        _LIMIT 64
                                        CLS
                                        PRINT "Enter a value between 0 and 1, with 1 being full volume"
                                        PRINT ": "; volume$
                                        pre = 1
                                        GOSUB controls
                                        IF k$ = CHR$(46) AND decimal = 0 THEN
                                            decimal = 1
                                            volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                            inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                            decimalloc = LEN(volume$)
                                        END IF
                                        IF k$ >= CHR$(48) AND k$ <= CHR$(58) THEN
                                            volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                            inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                        END IF
                                        IF k$ = CHR$(8) AND inputlength > 0 THEN
                                            volume$ = MID$(volume$, 1, (inputlength - 1))
                                            inputlength = (inputlength - 1)
                                            IF inputlength < decimalloc THEN
                                                decimal = 0
                                            END IF
                                        END IF
                                        _DISPLAY
                                    LOOP UNTIL k$ = CHR$(13)
                                    volume = VAL(volume$)
                                    IF volume < 0 OR volume > 1 THEN
                                        volume$ = ""
                                        inputlength = 0
                                        EXIT DO
                                    END IF
                                    _SNDVOL shufflejukebox, volume
                                    exitloop = 1
                                    EXIT DO
                                LOOP
                                IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                            LOOP
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(52) THEN
                            exitloop = 1
                            EXIT DO
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(53) AND nottheme = 0 THEN
                            theme$ = location$
                            filename$ = "user\pref\theme.txt"
                            userdata$ = location$
                            GOSUB encrypter
                            duotheme = 0
                            filename$ = "user\pref\duotheme.txt"
                            userdata$ = STR$(duotheme)
                            GOSUB encrypter
                            _SNDPAUSE shufflejukebox
                            GOTO PREBEGIN
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(54) THEN
                            GOTO PREBEGIN
                        END IF
                        playing = _SNDPLAYING(shufflejukebox)
                        IF playing = 0 AND pause = 0 THEN
                            exitloop = 1
                            EXIT DO
                        END IF
                        _DISPLAY
                    LOOP
                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                LOOP
            LOOP
        END IF
        IF k$ = CHR$(52) THEN
            GOTO PREBEGIN
        END IF
        IF k$ = CHR$(53) THEN
            DO
                _LIMIT 64
                CLS
                PRINT "Here you can take two songs and mix them together"
                PRINT "You can change the volume of each to make the perfect match"
                PRINT "Once you are done, you can listen to it or save it as your theme"
                PRINT "Press Space to begin"
                pre = 1
                GOSUB controls
                _DISPLAY
            LOOP UNTIL k$ = CHR$(32)
            DO
                volume1 = 0
                volume2 = 0
                song1$ = ""
                song2$ = ""
                location1$ = ""
                location2$ = ""
                exitloop = 0
                DO
                    _LIMIT 64
                    CLS
                    PRINT "How would you like to pick your songs?"
                    PRINT "     1-Pick new 2 songs"
                    PRINT "     2-Select a Duo from your favorites"
                    pre = 1
                    GOSUB controls
                    IF k$ = CHR$(49) THEN
                        DO
                            DO
                                _LIMIT 64
                                CLS
                                PRINT "Please pick your first song"
                                PRINT "Please select an album"
                                PRINT "-All music property of Nexon"
                                PRINT "     0-Give me a Random First Song"
                                PRINT "     1-Maple Island"
                                PRINT "     2-Victoria Island"
                                PRINT "     3-El Nath Mts."
                                PRINT "     4-Ludas Lake"
                                PRINT "     5-Nihal Desert"
                                PRINT "     6-Mu Lung Garden"
                                PRINT "     7-Minar Forest"
                                PRINT "     8-Aqua Road"
                                PRINT "     9-Edelstein"
                                PRINT "     a-Temple of Time"
                                PRINT "     b-Rein"
                                PRINT "     c-Ereve"
                                PRINT "     d-Travel"
                                PRINT "     e-Tour"
                                PRINT "     f-Event"
                                PRINT "     g-Other"
                                pre = 1
                                GOSUB controls
                                IF k$ = CHR$(48) THEN
                                    RANDOMIZE TIMER
                                    randomsongpick = INT(RND * 207)

                                        CASE 0

                                    location2$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\38.ogg"
                                CASE 201
                                    song2$ = "???"
                                    location2$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\39.ogg"
                                CASE 202
                                    song2$ = "???"
                                    location2$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\40.ogg"
                                CASE 203
                                    song2$ = "???"
                                    location2$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\41.ogg"
                                CASE 204
                                    song2$ = "???"
                                    location2$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\42.ogg"
                                CASE 205
                                    song2$ = "???"
                                    location2$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\43.ogg"
                                CASE 206
                                    song2$ = "???"
                                    location2$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\44.ogg"
                            END SELECT
                            volume1 = 1
                            volume2 = 1
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(53) THEN
                            exitloop = 0
                            DO
                                DO
                                    RANDOMIZE TIMER
                                    volume1 = (((RND * 10) + 1) / 10)
                                    IF volume1 > 1 OR volume1 < 0 THEN EXIT DO
                                    exitloop = 1
                                    EXIT DO
                                LOOP
                                IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                            LOOP
                            exitloop = 0
                            DO
                                DO
                                    RANDOMIZE TIMER
                                    volume2 = (((RND * 10) + 1) / 10)
                                    IF volume2 > 1 OR volume2 < 0 THEN EXIT DO
                                    exitloop = 1
                                    EXIT DO
                                LOOP
                                IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                            LOOP
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(54) THEN
                            exitloop = 0
                            filename$ = "user\mixer\fav1song1.txt"
                            GOSUB decrypter
                            fav1song1$ = userdata$
                            filename$ = "user\mixer\fav2song1.txt"
                            GOSUB decrypter
                            fav2song1$ = userdata$
                            filename$ = "user\mixer\fav3song1.txt"
                            GOSUB decrypter
                            fav3song1$ = userdata$
                            filename$ = "user\mixer\fav4song1.txt"
                            GOSUB decrypter
                            fav4song1$ = userdata$
                            filename$ = "user\mixer\fav5song1.txt"
                            GOSUB decrypter
                            fav5song1$ = userdata$
                            DO
                                _LIMIT 64
                                CLS
                                PRINT "Which slot would you like to set this Duo to?"
                                PRINT "     1-Slot 1"
                                PRINT "     2-Slot 2"
                                PRINT "     3-Slot 3"
                                PRINT "     4-Slot 4"
                                PRINT "     5-Slot 5"
                                pre = 1
                                GOSUB controls
                                IF k$ = CHR$(49) THEN
                                    IF fav1song1$ <> "0" THEN
                                        DO
                                            _LIMIT 64
                                            CLS
                                            PRINT "You already have a Duo set to this slot!"
                                            PRINT "Are you sure you want to overwrite it?"
                                            PRINT "     y-Yes"
                                            PRINT "     n-No"
                                            pre = 1
                                            GOSUB controls
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(121) THEN
                                                EXIT DO
                                            END IF
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(110) THEN
                                                exitloop = 1
                                                EXIT DO
                                            END IF
                                            _DISPLAY
                                        LOOP
                                    END IF
                                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav1song1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = song1$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav1song2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = song2$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav1loc1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location1$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav1loc2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location2$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav1vol1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume1)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav1vol2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume2)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    EXIT DO
                                END IF
                                IF k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
                                    IF fav2song1$ <> "0" THEN
                                        DO
                                            _LIMIT 64
                                            CLS
                                            PRINT "You already have a Duo set to this slot!"
                                            PRINT "Are you sure you want to overwrite it?"
                                            PRINT "     y-Yes"
                                            PRINT "     n-No"
                                            pre = 1
                                            GOSUB controls
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(121) THEN
                                                EXIT DO
                                            END IF
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(110) THEN
                                                exitloop = 1
                                                EXIT DO
                                            END IF
                                            _DISPLAY
                                        LOOP
                                    END IF
                                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav2song1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = song1$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav2song2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = song2$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav2loc1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location1$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav2loc2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location2$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav2vol1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume1)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav2vol2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume2)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    EXIT DO
                                END IF
                                IF k$ = CHR$(51) THEN
                                    IF fav1song3$ <> "0" THEN
                                        DO
                                            _LIMIT 64
                                            CLS
                                            PRINT "You already have a Duo set to this slot!"
                                            PRINT "Are you sure you want to overwrite it?"

                                            pre = 1

                                            IF k$ = CHR$(121) THEN

                                                exitloop = 1
                                                EXIT DO
                                            END IF
                                            _DISPLAY
                                        LOOP
                                    END IF
                                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav3song1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = song1$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav3song2.txt"

                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav3loc1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location1$
                                    GOSUB encrypter

                                    userdata$ = location2$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav3vol1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume1)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav3vol2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume2)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    EXIT DO
                                END IF
                                IF k$ = CHR$(52) THEN
                                    IF fav1song4$ <> "0" THEN
                                        DO
                                            _LIMIT 64
                                            CLS
                                            PRINT "You already have a Duo set to this slot!"
                                            PRINT "Are you sure you want to overwrite it?"
                                            PRINT "     y-Yes"

                                            pre = 1
                                            GOSUB controls
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(121) THEN

                                            _DISPLAY

                                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav4song1.txt"

                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav4loc1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location1$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav4loc2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location2$
                                    GOSUB encrypter

                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume1)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav4vol2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume2)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    EXIT DO
                                END IF
                                IF k$ = CHR$(53) THEN
                                    IF fav1song5$ <> "0" THEN
                                        DO
                                            _LIMIT 64

                                    END IF
                                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav5song1.txt"

                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav5song2.txt"

                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav5loc2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = location2$
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav5vol1.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume1)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    filename$ = "user\mixer\fav5vol2.txt"
                                    userdata$ = STR$(volume2)
                                    GOSUB encrypter
                                    EXIT DO
                                END IF
                                _DISPLAY
                            LOOP
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(55) THEN
                            GOTO PREBEGIN
                        END IF
                        _DISPLAY
                    LOOP
                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                LOOP
            LOOP
        END IF
        IF k$ = CHR$(54) THEN
            OPEN "source\program\nous.txt" FOR INPUT AS #1
            INPUT #1, nous
            CLOSE #1
            DO
                _SNDCLOSE jukeboxunkown
                exitloop = 0
                selecttype = 0
                DO
                    _LIMIT 64
                    CLS
                    PRINT "In this section you will be able to help this program grow"
                    PRINT "I don't know where in the Maple World these songs are from"
                    PRINT "If you know where a song is from, please contact me"
                    PRINT "There are currently"; nous; "unknown songs"
                    PRINT "What would you like to do"
                    PRINT "     1-Select an Unkown Song by number"
                    PRINT "     2-Listen to a random Unknown Song"
                    pre = 1
                    GOSUB controls
                    IF k$ = CHR$(49) OR k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
                        IF k$ = CHR$(49) THEN
                            selecttype = 1
                        END IF
                        IF k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
                            selecttype = 2
                        END IF
                        DO
                            IF selecttype = 1 THEN
                                unknownsong$ = ""
                                inputlength = 0
                                DO
                                    DO
                                        DO
                                            _LIMIT 64
                                            CLS
                                            PRINT "Enter a number from 1 to"; nous
                                            PRINT ": "; unknownsong$
                                            pre = 1
                                            GOSUB controls
                                            IF k$ >= CHR$(48) AND k$ <= CHR$(57) THEN
                                                unknownsong$ = unknownsong$ + k$
                                                inputlength = LEN(unknownsong$)
                                            END IF
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(8) AND inputlength > 0 THEN
                                                unknownsong$ = MID$(unknownsong$, 1, (inputlength - 1))
                                                inputlength = (inputlength - 1)
                                            END IF
                                            IF inputlength > 2 THEN
                                                unknownsong$ = MID$(unknownsong$, 1, 2)
                                                inputlength = 2
                                            END IF
                                            _DISPLAY
                                        LOOP UNTIL k$ = CHR$(13)
                                        unknownsong = VAL(unknownsong$)
                                        IF unknownsong < 1 OR unknownsong > nous THEN
                                            unknownsong$ = ""
                                            inputlength = 0
                                            EXIT DO
                                        END IF
                                        exitloop = 1
                                        EXIT DO
                                    LOOP
                                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                                LOOP
                            END IF
                            IF selecttype = 2 THEN
                                RANDOMIZE TIMER
                                unknownsong = INT(RND * 44 + 1)
                            END IF
                            SELECT CASE unknownsong
                                CASE 1
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\01.ogg"
                                CASE 2
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\02.ogg"
                                CASE 3
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\03.ogg"
                                CASE 4
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\04.ogg"
                                CASE 5
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\05.ogg"
                                CASE 6
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\06.ogg"
                                CASE 7
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\07.ogg"
                                CASE 8
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\08.ogg"
                                CASE 9
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\09.ogg"
                                CASE 10
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\10.ogg"
                                CASE 11
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\11.ogg"
                                CASE 12
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\12.ogg"
                                CASE 13
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\13.ogg"
                                CASE 14
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\14.ogg"
                                CASE 15
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\15.ogg"
                                CASE 16
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\16.ogg"
                                CASE 17
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\17.ogg"
                                CASE 18
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\18.ogg"
                                CASE 19
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\19.ogg"
                                CASE 20
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\20.ogg"
                                CASE 21
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\21.ogg"
                                CASE 22
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\22.ogg"
                                CASE 23
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\23.ogg"
                                CASE 24
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\24.ogg"
                                CASE 25
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\25.ogg"
                                CASE 26
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\26.ogg"
                                CASE 27
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\27.ogg"
                                CASE 28
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\28.ogg"
                                CASE 29
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\29.ogg"
                                CASE 30
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\30.ogg"
                                CASE 31
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\31.ogg"
                                CASE 32
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\32.ogg"
                                CASE 33
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\33.ogg"
                                CASE 34
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\34.ogg"
                                CASE 35
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\35.ogg"
                                CASE 36
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\36.ogg"
                                CASE 37
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\37.ogg"
                                CASE 38
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\38.ogg"
                                CASE 39
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\39.ogg"
                                CASE 40
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\40.ogg"
                                CASE 41
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\41.ogg"
                                CASE 42
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\42.ogg"
                                CASE 43
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\43.ogg"
                                CASE 44
                                    location$ = "audio\UNKNOWN\44.ogg"
                            END SELECT
                            EXIT DO
                        LOOP
                        jukeboxunknown = _SNDOPEN(location$, "VOL, SYNC, LEN, PAUSE")
                        _SNDPLAY jukeboxunknown
                        DO
                            _LIMIT 64
                            CLS
                            PRINT " You are are currently listening to"; unknownsong; "!"
                            length = _SNDLEN(jukeboxunknown)
                            minutes = INT((length / 60))
                            minutes$ = STR$(minutes)
                            minutes$ = LTRIM$(minutes$)
                            seconds = INT((length - (minutes * 60)))
                            seconds$ = STR$(seconds)
                            seconds$ = LTRIM$(seconds$)
                            digitseconds = LEN(seconds$)
                            IF digitseconds = 1 THEN
                                seconds$ = "0" + seconds$
                            END IF
                            position = _SNDGETPOS(jukeboxunknown)
                            playingminutes = INT((position / 60))
                            playingminutes$ = STR$(playingminutes)
                            playingminutes$ = LTRIM$(playingminutes$)
                            playingseconds = INT((position - (playingminutes * 60)))
                            playingseconds$ = STR$(playingseconds)
                            playingseconds$ = LTRIM$(playingseconds$)
                            playingdigitseconds = LEN(playingseconds$)
                            IF playingdigitseconds = 1 THEN
                                playingseconds$ = "0" + playingseconds$
                            END IF
                            timedisplay$ = " " + playingminutes$ + ":" + playingseconds$
                            totaltime$ = minutes$ + ":" + seconds$
                            PSET (10, 25)
                            DRAW "D14 R200 U14 L200"
                            barloc = _ROUND(((position / length) * 197))
                            PSET ((barloc + 10), 31)
                            PSET ((barloc + 10), 32)
                            PSET ((barloc + 10), 33)
                            PSET ((barloc + 11), 31)
                            PSET ((barloc + 11), 32)
                            PSET ((barloc + 11), 33)
                            PSET ((barloc + 12), 31)
                            PSET ((barloc + 12), 32)
                            PSET ((barloc + 12), 33)
                            LOCATE 4, 2
                            PRINT timedisplay$
                            LOCATE 4, 23
                            PRINT totaltime$
                            PRINT
                            PRINT "What would you like to do?"
                            PRINT "     1-Pause song"
                            PRINT "     2-Play song"
                            PRINT "     3-Change Volume"
                            PRINT "     4-Make this song your theme"
                            PRINT "     5-Play new song"
                            PRINT "     6-Exit"
                            pre = 1
                            GOSUB controls
                            IF k$ = CHR$(49) THEN
                                _SNDPAUSE jukeboxunknown
                            END IF
                            IF k$ = CHR$(50) THEN
                                playing = _SNDPLAYING(jukeboxunknown)
                                IF playing = 0 THEN
                                    _SNDPLAY jukeboxunknown
                                END IF
                            END IF
                            IF k$ = CHR$(51) THEN
                                volume$ = ""
                                DO
                                    decimal = 0
                                    DO
                                        DO
                                            _LIMIT 64
                                            CLS
                                            PRINT "Enter a value between 0 and 1, with 1 being full volume"
                                            PRINT ": "; volume$
                                            pre = 1
                                            GOSUB controls
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(46) AND decimal = 0 THEN
                                                decimal = 1
                                                volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                                inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                                decimalloc = LEN(volume$)
                                            END IF
                                            IF k$ >= CHR$(48) AND k$ <= CHR$(58) THEN
                                                volume$ = volume$ + k$
                                                inputlength = LEN(volume$)
                                            END IF
                                            IF k$ = CHR$(8) AND inputlength > 0 THEN
                                                volume$ = MID$(volume$, 1, (inputlength - 1))
                                                inputlength = (inputlength - 1)
                                                IF inputlength < decimalloc THEN
                                                    decimal = 0
                                                END IF
                                            END IF
                                            _DISPLAY
                                        LOOP UNTIL k$ = CHR$(13)
                                        volume = VAL(volume$)
                                        IF volume < 0 OR volume > 1 THEN
                                            volume$ = ""
                                            inputlength = 0
                                            EXIT DO
                                        END IF
                                        _SNDVOL jukeboxunknown, volume
                                        exitloop = 1
                                        EXIT DO
                                    LOOP
                                    IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                                LOOP
                                exitloop = 0
                            END IF
                            IF k$ = CHR$(52) AND nottheme = 0 THEN
                                theme$ = location$
                                filename$ = "user\pref\theme.txt"
                                userdata$ = location$
                                GOSUB encrypter
                                duotheme = 0
                                filename$ = "user\pref\duotheme.txt"
                                userdata$ = STR$(duotheme)
                                GOSUB encrypter
                                _SNDPAUSE jukeboxunknown
                                GOTO PREBEGIN
                            END IF
                            IF k$ = CHR$(53) THEN
                                _SNDPAUSE jukeboxunknown
                                exitloop = 1
                                EXIT DO
                            END IF
                            IF k$ = CHR$(54) THEN
                                GOTO PREBEGIN
                            END IF
                            _DISPLAY
                        LOOP
                        IF exitloop = 1 THEN EXIT DO
                    END IF
                    _DISPLAY
                LOOP
            LOOP
        END IF
        _DISPLAY
    LOOP
END IF
